{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1}
yajñaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 1]
sa trayāṇāṃ varṇānām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 2]
brāhmaṇakṣatriyayor vaiśyasya ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 3]
asaṃyujya vidhīyamānaṃ sādhāraṇam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 4]
saṃyogād vyavatiṣṭhate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 5]
yajñopavītī devakarmāṇi karoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 6]
prācīnāpavītī pitryāṇi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 7]
ācamanaprabhṛti yenādhikaraṇena saṃyujyeta na tena vyāvarteta | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 8]
na ca vyaveyāt | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 9]
ity āvṛtāṃ lakṣaṇā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 10]
uddeśaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 11]
uttarata upācāraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 12]
prāṅnyāyāni devakarmāṇi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 13]
dakṣiṇānyāyāni pitryāṇi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 14]
āsīnanyāyam bāhvṛcyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 15]
vacanāt sthānam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 16]
hotā ca kuryād anādiṣṭam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 17]
triprabhṛtiṣv ṛggaṇeṣu prathamottamayos trir vacanam anyatra japebhyaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 18]
uttamasya ca chandomānasya ūrdhvam ādivyañjanāt sthāna oṃkāraḥ plutas trimātraḥ śuddhaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 19]
makārānto vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 20]
taṃ praṇava ity ācakṣate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 21]
avasāne makārāntaṃ sarveṣv ṛggaṇeṣu sapuronuvākyeṣu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 22]
tenārdharcam uttarasyāḥ saṃdhāyāvasyati pādaṃ vā tat saṃtatam ity ācakṣate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 23]
sa sarveṣām ṛggaṇānāṃ dharmo ye karmasaṃyogena codyante | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 24]
vidūreṣv api karmasv antareṇa prathamāṃ paridhānīyām ca saṃtānārtho 'rdharcena kāṅkṣati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 25]
ardharcanyāyāś carcaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 26]
vacanād anyat | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 27]
uccairnyāyaś cargvedaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 28]
vacanād upāṃśutā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 29]
saṃsvāranyāyatā ca śabdānām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 30]
aikasvaryaṃ ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 31]
uccaistarāṃ praṇavaḥ puronuvākyāyāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 32]
praṇavād yājyā uccaistarām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 33]
uccaistarām vaṣaṭkāraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 34]
samo vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 35]
praṇavo ye yajāmahe vaṣaṭkāraḥ saṃpraiṣāḥ praiṣāś ca uccair upāṃśu haviḥṣu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 36]
devatānāmadheyaṃ ca upāṃśu nigamasthāneṣu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 37]
bhūr bhuva iti purastāj japaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 38]
ye yajāmahe vauṣaḍ ojaḥ sahaḥ saha ojaḥ svar ity upariṣṭād iti catuṣṭayaṃ sarvāsu yājyāsu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 39]
anuyājeṣu tu ye yajāmahe nāsti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 40]
anuvaṣaṭkāre ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 41]
plutena yājyāntena vaṣaṭkārasya saṃdhānam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 42]
aplutena vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 43]
tad upāṃśuyāje nāsti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 1 44]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2}
plāvayed ākāram āvāhanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 1]
yeyajāmahaḥ plutādiḥ purastād yājyānām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 2]
caturmātrā yājñikī plutiḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 3]
saṃdhyakṣarāṇāṃ tālusthāne ā3ikārī bhavataḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 4]
oṣṭhyasthāne ā3ukārī bhavataḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 5]
anyāni prakṛtyākṣarāṇi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 6]
ekāraukārau ca pragṛhyau | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 7]
yājyānte | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 8]
visarjanīyo riphito repham āpadyate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 9]
lupyate 'riphitaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 10]
anusvāraṃ makāraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 11]
anyāni prakṛtyā vyañjanāni | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 12]
aukāro vaṣaṭkāre caturmātraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 13]
ṣakārācca uttaro 'kāraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 14]
prakṛtyā vobhau | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 15]
pūrvo vā prakṛtyā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 16]
prakṛtyākāra iti jātūkarṇyaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 17]
bārhatarāthantaraṃ vaṣaṭkuryāt purastāddīrgham upariṣṭāddhrasvam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 18]
upariṣṭācca yeyajāmahād devatādeśanaṃ sapuronuvākye | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 19]
sapraiṣe tu na vidyate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 20]
juhotīty ukte sarpiḥ pratīyeta | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 21]
svāhākāro 'nte homamantrāṇām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 22]
samidādhānamantrāṇāṃ ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 23]
mantrapṛthaktvāt karmapṛthaktvam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 24]
itikaraṇaś ca mantrānte | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 25]
mantrāntena karaṇeṣu karmaṇaḥ saṃnipātanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 26]
saṃpreṣito 'nvāha | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 27]
tathā yajati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 28]
ity etat sārvayajñikam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 2 29]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3}
upoṣya paurṇamāsena haviṣā yajate tathā āmāvāsyena | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718530_1]
dve paurṇamāsyau amāvāsye ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718532_1]
yām pari astamayam pūrṇaḥ udiyāt yām ca astamite te paurṇamāsyau | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718534_1]
śvas na draṣṭā iti yat ahar ca na dṛśyeta te amāvāsye | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718535_1]
tatrejyāyām yāthākāmī | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 7]
iti paurṇamāsyām iti amāvāsyāyām iti upadeśāt vyavatiṣṭhante | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718537_1]
tad saṃyuktāḥ ca śabdāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718538_1]
samānam anyat | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718539_1]
ubhayatra āgneyaḥ puroḍāśaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718540_1]
agnīṣomīyaḥ upāṃśuyājaḥ vaiṣṇavaḥ vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718541_1]
aindrāgnaḥ a saṃnayataḥ dvitīyaḥ amāvāsyāyām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718543_1]
aindram sāṃnāyyam saṃnayataḥ māhendram vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 718544_1]
vaiṣṇavaṃ tv asaṃnayann upāṃśuyājam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 3 17]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4}
āmantrito hotāntareṇotkaraṃ praṇītāś ca pratipadya dakṣiṇena prapadena barhirākramaṇam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 1]
vedyantasaṃmitā paścātpārṣṇiḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 2]
vikramya ca sthānam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 3]
agnaye samidhyamānāyeti saṃpreṣitaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 4]
kaṃ prapadye taṃ prapadye yat te prajāpate śaraṇaṃ chandas tat prapadye yāvat te viṣṇo veda tāvat te kariṣyāmi devena savitā prasūta ārtvijyam kariṣyāmi namo 'gnaye upadraṣṭre namo vāyava upaśrotre nama ādityāya anukhyātre juṣṭām adya devebhyo vācaṃ vadiṣyāmi śuśrūṣeṇyāṃ manuṣyebhyaḥ svadhāvatīṃ pitṛbhyaḥ pratiṣṭhāṃ viśvasmai bhūtāya praśāsta ātmanā prajayā paśubhiḥ prajāpatiṃ prapadye 'bhayaṃ no 'stu prājāpatyam anuvakṣyāmi vāg ārtvijyam kariṣyati vācaṃ prapadye bhūr bhuvaḥ svar iti japitvā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 5]
trir hiṃkṛtya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 6]
pra vo vājā ity upasaṃdhāya madhyamayā vācā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 7]
agna ā yāhi vītaya īḍenya iti tṛcau | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 8]
agniṃ dūtaṃ vṛṇīmaha ity ekā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 9]
samidhyamāno 'dhvara ity ekā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 10]
tisraḥ sāptadaśye | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 11]
tad anyatra sāyanābhyāṃ darśapūrṇamāsābhyām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 12]
samiddho 'gna āhuteti dve | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 13]
agne mahān asi brāhmaṇa bhārateti praṇavena saṃdhāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 14]
amuto 'rvāñci yajamānasya trīṇyārṣeyāṇy abhivyāhṛtya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 15]
ṣaṭ tu dvigotrasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 16]
purohitapravareṇābrāhmaṇasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 17]
mānaveti vā sarveṣām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 18]
deveddho manviddha ṛṣiṣṭuto viprānumaditaḥ kaviśasto brahmasaṃśito ghṛtāhavana ity avasāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 19]
praṇīr yajñānāṃ rathīr adhvarāṇām atūrto hotā tūrṇir havyavāḍ ity avasāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 20]
āspātram juhūr devānāṃ camaso devapāno 'rāṁ iva agne nemir devāṃstvaṃ paribhūr asi ity avasāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 21]
vyavasyann āvāhayati devatāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 4 22]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5}
āvaha devān yajamānāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5 1]
agnim agna āvaha somam āvahety ājyabhāgau | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5 2]
agnim āvahāgnīṣomāvāvaha viṣṇuṃ vā agnīṣomāvāvahendrāgnī āvahendram āvaha mahendraṃ vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5 3]
devān ājyapān āvaha | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5 4]
agniṃ hotrāyāvaha | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5 5]
svaṃ mahimānam āvaha | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5 6]
ā ca vaha jātavedaḥ suyajā ca yajety āvāhya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5 7]
upaviśyordhvajānur dakṣiṇena prādeśena bhūmim anvārabhya japati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5 8]
asyai pratiṣṭhāyai mā chitsi pṛthivi mātar mā mā hiṃsīr mā modoṣīr madhu maniṣye madhu vaniṣye madhu janiṣye madhumatīm adya devebhyo vācaṃ vadiṣyāmi cāruṃ manuṣyebhya idam ahaṃ pañcadaśena vajreṇa pāpmānam bhrātṛvyam avabādha iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5 9.1]
saptadaśena vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 5 9.2]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6}
mānuṣa ity uktaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 1]
deva savitar etaṃ tvā vṛṇate saha pitrā vaiśvānareṇendra pūṣan bṛhaspate pra ca vada pra ca yaja vasūnāṃ rātau syāma rudrāṇām omyāyāṃ svādityā ādityā anehaso yad asya hotṛvūrye jihmaṃ cakṣuḥ parāpatāt | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 2.1]
agniṣṭat punar ābharāj jātavedā vicarṣaṇir iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 2.2]
pravṛto japitvā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 2.3]
upotthāyādhvaryor dakṣiṇena prādeśena dakṣiṇam aṃsam anvārabhya japati savyena agnīdho dakṣiṇam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 3.1]
indram anvārabhāmahe hotṛvūrye purohitam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 3.2]
yenāyann uttamaṃ svar devā aṅgiraso divam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 3.3]
ṣaṣṭiśca adhvaryū navatiśca pāśā antarā dyāvāpṛthivī vicṛttāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 3.4]
sinanti pākam adhi dhīra emi syone me dyāvāpṛthivī ubhe ime | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 3.5]
iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 3.6]
ṣaṇ morvīr aṃhasaḥ pāntu dyauś ca pṛthivī cāhaś ca rātriś cāpaś cauṣadhayaścetyavasṛjya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 4]
aindrīm āvṛtam āvarta ādityasya āvṛtam anvāvarta iti dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anvāvṛtya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 5]
nirastaḥ parāvasur yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmas tena saheti hotṛṣadanāt śuṣkaṃ tṛṇam ubhayataḥ praticchidya dakṣiṇāparam avāntaradeśaṃ nirasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 6]
apa upaspṛśya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 7]
aśuṣkam udagagraṃ nidhāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 8]
idam aham arvāvasoḥ sadasi sīdāmīty upaviśya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 9]
dakṣiṇottaram upastham kṛtvā prāñcau pāṇī pragṛhya japati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 10]
namo dyāvāpṛthivībhyāṃ hotṛbhyāṃ pūrvasūbhyāṃ viśvakarmāṇau tanūpau me sthas tanvaṃ me pātaṃ mā mā hiṃsiṣṭaṃ mā mā saṃtāptam ity āhavanīyaṃ prekṣya gārhapatyaṃ ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 11]
udak saṃsarpann āhaiṣa vām ākāśa iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 12]
viśve devāḥ śāstana tad adya vāco namo mahadbhya iti japitvā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 13]
agnir hotā vettu agnir hotraṃ vettu prāvitraṃ sādhu te yajamāna devatety avasāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 14]
yo 'gniṃ hotāram avṛthā ity upāṃśu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 15]
ghṛtavatīm adhvaryo srucam āsyasva devayuvaṃ viśvavārām īḍāmahai devān īḍe 'nyān namasyāma namasyān yajāma yajñiyān iti sruvāv ādāpya pañca prayājān yajati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 6 16]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 7}
samidhaḥ samidho 'gna ājyasya vyantv iti prathamaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 7 1]
ājyasya vetv iti dvitīyaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 7 2]
narāśaṃso 'gna ājyasya vetv iti dvitīyo vasiṣṭhaśunakānām atrivadhryaśvānāṃ kaṇvasaṃkṛtīnāṃ rājanyānāṃ prajākāmānāṃ ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 7 3]

barhir agna ājyasya vetv iti caturthaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 7 5]
svāhāgniṃ svāhā somaṃ svāhāgniṃ svāhāgnīṣomau viṣṇuṃ vā svāhā agnīṣomau svāhendrāgnī svāhendraṃ mahendraṃ vā svāhā devā ājyapā juṣāṇā agna ājyasya haviṣo vyantv iti prayājayājyāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 7 6]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 8}

bhuvo yajñasyeti yājyā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 8 5]

endra sānasiṃ pra sasāhiṣa iti sāṃnāyyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 8 12]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 9}
piprīhi devān iti sviṣṭakṛtaḥ puronuvākyā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 9 1]
ayāḍ agnir agneḥ priyā dhāmāny ayāṭ somasya priyā dhāmāny ayāḍ agneḥ priyā dhāmāny ayāḍ agnīṣomayoḥ priyā dhāmāni viṣṇor vāyāḍ agnīṣomayoḥ priyā dhāmāny ayāḍ indrāgnyoḥ priyā dhāmāny ayāḍ indrasya priyā dhāmāni mahendrasya vāyāḍ devānām ājyapānāṃ priyā dhāmāni yakṣad agner hotuḥ priyā dhāmāni yakṣat svaṃ mahimānam āyajatām ejyā iṣaḥ kṛṇotu so 'dhvarā jātavedā juṣatāṃ havir agne yad adya viśo 'dhvarasyeti yājyā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 9 2]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 10}
iḍām upahvāsyamānasya dakṣiṇasya pāṇeḥ pradeśinyām anakti uttame ca parvaṇi madhyame ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 10 718625_1]
vācaspatinā te hutasya prāśnāmi iṣe prāṇāya iti pūrvam añjanam adhare oṣṭhe nilipyati manasaspatinā te hutasya prāśnāmi ūrje udānāya iti uttara oṣṭhe uttaram | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 10 718627_1]
upaspṛśya dakṣiṇena uttara iḍām dhārayan a prasāritābhiḥ aṅgulibhiḥ a muṣṭi kṛtābhiḥ svayam pañcamam ādāya mukha saṃmitām dhārayan hṛdaya saṃmitām vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 10 718629_1]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11}
upahūtaṃ bṛhat saha divā saha sūryeṇa saha cakṣuṣā upa māṃ bṛhat saha divā saha sūryeṇa saha cakṣuṣā hvayatām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 1.1]
upahūtaṃ vāmadevyaṃ sahāntarikṣeṇa saha vāyunā saha prāṇenopa māṃ vāmadevyaṃ sahāntarikṣeṇa saha vāyunā saha prāṇena hvayatām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 1.2]
upahūtaṃ rathantaraṃ saha pṛthivyā sahāgninā saha vācā saha paśubhir upa māṃ rathantaraṃ saha pṛthivyā sahāgninā saha vācā saha paśubhir hvayatām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 2]
upahūtaṃ sthāsnu bhuvanam upa māṃ sthāsnu bhuvanaṃ hvayatām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 3]
upahūtaṃ cariṣṇu bhuvanam upa māṃ cariṣṇu bhuvanaṃ hvayatām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 4.1]
upahūtaḥ sakhā bhakṣa upa māṃ sakhā bhakṣo hvayatām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 4.2]
upahūtāḥ sapta hotrā upa māṃ sapta hotrā hvayantām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 5.1]
upahūtā gāvaḥ sahāśiropa māṃ gāvaḥ sahāśirā hvayantām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 5.2]
upahūtā vāk saha prāṇenopa māṃ vāk saha prāṇena hvayatām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 6.1]
upahūtā vāk saha manasopa māṃ vāk saha manasā hvayatām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 6.2]
upahūteḍā vṛṣṭir upa mām iḍā vṛṣṭir hvayatām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 7.1]
upahūteḍā taturir upa mām iḍā taturir hvayatām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 7.2]
upahūtā he sāsi juṣasva meḍa iti japitvā iḍām upahvayate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 11 7.3]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12}
iḍopahūtopahūteḍopāsmān iḍā hvayatām iḍopahūtā mānavī ghṛtapadī maitrāvaruṇī | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 1]
brahma devakṛtam upahūtam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 2.1]
daivyā adhvaryava upahūtā upahūtā manuṣyā ya imam yajñam avānye ca yajñapatiṃ vardhān | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 2.2]
upahūte dyāvāpṛthivī pūrvaje ṛtāvarī devī devaputre | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 2.3]
upahūto 'yam yajamāna uttarasyāṃ devayajyāyām upahūto bhūyasi haviṣkaraṇa idaṃ me devā havir juṣantām iti tasminn upahūta ity upahūya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 3]
avaghrāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 4]
antariḍaṃ catur avāniti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 5]
ante vā caturtham | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 6]
iḍāsi syonāsi syonakṛt sā naḥ suprajāstve rāyaspoṣe dhāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 7.1]
juṣṭe juṣṭiṃ te gameyopahūta upahavaṃ te 'śīya mukhasya tvā dyumnāya surabhyāsyatvāya prāśnāmīty uttareḍāṃ prāśya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 7.2]
itarām yajamānapañcamāḥ prāśya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 8]
ā mārjanād vāgyamanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 9]
idam āpa iti tṛcenāntarvedi pavitravati mārjayante | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 10]
parihṛte brahmabhāge 'nvāhāryam āharanti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 11]
eṣa dakṣiṇākālaḥ sarvāsām iṣṭīnām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 12]
nānvāhāryo 'sty ādiṣṭadakṣiṇāsu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 13]
eṣā te 'gne samit tayā vardhasva cā ca pyāyasva | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 14.1]
vardhiṣīmahi ca vayam ā ca pyāsiṣīmahi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 14.2]
iti samidham anumantrya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 14.3]
trīn anuyājān yajati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 12 15]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 13}
devaṃ barhir vasuvane vasudheyasya vetu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 13 1]
devo narāśaṃso vasuvane vasudheyasya vetu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 13 2]
devo 'gniḥ sviṣṭakṛt sudraviṇā mandraḥ kaviḥ satyamanmā āyajī hotā hotur hotur āyajīyān agne yān devān ayāḍ yān apiprer ye te hotre 'matsatety avasāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 13 3]
tāṃ sasanuṣīṃ hotrāṃ devaṃgamāṃ divi deveṣu yajñam erayemaṃ sviṣṭakṛccāgne hotā bhūr vasuvane vasudheyasya namovāke vīhīty anuyājayājyāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 13 4]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14}
sūktā brūhīty uktaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 1]
idaṃ dyāvāpṛthivī bhadram abhūd ārdhma sūktavākam uta namovākam ṛdhyāsma sūktocyam agne tvaṃ sūktavāg asīty avasāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 2]
upaśrutī divaspṛthivyor omanvatī te 'smin yajñe yajamāna dyāvāpṛthivī stām ity avasāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 3]
śaṃgayī jīradānū atrasnū apravede urugavyūtī abhayam kṛtāv ity avasāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 4]
vṛṣṭidyāvā rītyāpā śambhuvau mayobhuvā ūrjasvatī payasvatī sūpacaraṇā ca svadhicaraṇā ca tayor āvidīty avasāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 5]
agnir havir ajuṣata avīvṛdhata maho jyāyo 'kṛta | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 6]
somo havir ajuṣata avīvṛdhata maho jyāyo 'kṛta | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 7]
agnir havir ajuṣatāvīvṛdhata maho jyāyo 'kṛta | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 8]
agnīṣomau havir ajuṣetām avīvṛdhetāṃ maho jyāyo 'krātām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 9]
viṣṇur vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 10]
agnīṣomau havir ajuṣetām avīvṛdhetāṃ maho jyāyo 'krātām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 11]
indrāgnī havir ajuṣetām avīvṛdhetāṃ maho jyāyo 'krātām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 12]
indro havir ajuṣata avīvṛdhata maho jyāyo 'kṛta | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 13.1]
mahendro vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 13.2]
devā ājyapā ājyam ajuṣanta avīvṛdhanta maho jyāyo 'krata | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 14]
agnir hotreṇa havir ajuṣata avīvṛdhata maho jyāyo 'kṛta | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 15]
asyām ṛdhaddhotrāyāṃ devaṃgamāyām āśāste 'yam yajamānaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 16]
asāv asāv iti nāmanī yajamānasya abhivyāhṛtya uttarāṃ devayajyām āśāste bhūyo haviṣkaraṇam āśāsta āyur āśāste suprajāstvam āśāste divyaṃ dhāma āśāste | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 17]
yad anena haviṣāśāste tad aśyāt tad ṛdhyāt tad asmai devā rāsantāṃ tad agnir devo devebhyo vanutāṃ vayam agneḥ pari mānuṣāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 18]
iṣṭaṃ ca vītaṃ cābhūd ubhe cainam dyāvāpṛthivī aṃhasaḥ pātām eha gatir vām asyedaṃ ca namo devebhya iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 19]
nama upeti barhiṣy añjaliṃ nidhāya japati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 20]
śaṃyor brūhīty uktas tacchaṃyor iti śaṃyorvākam uktvopaspṛśya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 21]
srugādāpanādi mandrayājyabhāgāntam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 22]
paraṃ madhyamayā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 23]
anuyājādyuttamayā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 14 24]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15}
upāṃśu gārhapatye patnīsaṃyājaiś caranti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 1]
somaṃ tvaṣṭāraṃ devānāṃ patnīr agniṃ gṛhapatim iti yajati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 2]
rākāsinīvālyau prajākāmasya pūrve gṛhapateḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 3]
āpyāyasva saṃ te payāṃsīha tvaṣṭāraṃ tannas turīpaṃ devānāṃ patnīr uta gnā vyantu rākām aham yās te rāke sinīvāli yāsu bāhur agnir hotā gṛhapatir vayam u tvā gṛhapata iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 4]
yathā ha tyad vasava iti japitveḍām upahvayate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 5]
upahūteyaṃ yajamānīti vā vikāraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 6]
iḍāntāḥ patnīsaṃyājāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 7]
śaṃyvantā vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 8]
pra tvā muñcāmīti vedaṃ vimucya yoktram | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 9]
añjalau patnyāḥ kṛtvā vedaṃ ca muktam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 10]
adbhir veda yoktre pariṣiñcan japati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 11]
kāmāya tvā vedo 'si yena tvaṃ veda devebhyo vedo 'bhavas tenāsmabhyaṃ veda edhi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 12.1]
vedo 'si vittir asi videyam karmāsi karaṇam asi kriyāsaṃ sanir asi sanitāsi saneyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 12.2]
ghṛtavantam kulāyinaṃ rāyaspoṣaṃ sahasriṇam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 13.1]
vedo dadātu vājinam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 13.2]
iti vede patnīṃ vācayati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 13.3]
sa tṛṇāni pragṛhyāntareṇorū nyasyate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 14]
tantuṃ tanvann ity uttareṇa gārhapatyam ā barhiṣaḥ stīrtvā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 15]
āpṛṇo 'si sampṛṇaḥ prajayā mā paśubhir āpṛṇeti vedaśeṣam upasthāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 16]
etenāgne brahmaṇāyāḍ yajñam jātavedā antaraḥ pūrvo 'smin niṣadya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 17.1]
sanvan saniṃ suvimucā vimuñca dhehyasmabhyaṃ draviṇam jātavedaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 17.2]
ity āhavanīyam upasthāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 17.3]
upaspṛśyotsṛjyate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 15 18]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16}
vyākhyātau darśa pūrṇamāsau prakṛtiḥ iṣṭi paśubandhānām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718719_1]
anvayasya prakṛtiḥ iti ākhyā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718720_1]
antareṇa ājyabhāgau sviṣṭakṛtam ca yat ijyate tam āvāpaḥ iti ācakṣate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718721_1]
tat pradhānam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718721_2]
tad aṅgāni itarāṇi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718722_1]
teṣām a bhinna kāle arthe vibhavaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718723_1]
tantra lakṣaṇam tat | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718724_1]
pradānam uccāvacābhiḥ devatābhiḥ saṃyujya śrūyate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718725_1]
tatra devatā vikāre tad devate yājyā puronuvākye | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718726_1]
nigama sthāneṣu ca sā devatā upalakṣyate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718727_1]
āvāhane uttame prayāje sviṣṭakṛt nigade sūktavāke ca ijyamānāḥ devatāḥ nigacchanti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718728_1]
tasmāt nigama sthānāni | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718728_2]
anukrāmantaḥ ca vikārān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718729_1]
paurṇamāsī vikāraḥ iti ukte vārtraghnau pratīyāt amāvāsyā vikāraḥ iti vṛdhanvantau | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718730_1]
anādeśe vikalpa bhūtau devatātaḥ haviṣṭaḥ vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718732_1]
saṃnipāte haviṣṭaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718735_1]
sāmānyāt niyamaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718736_1]
sāptadaśyam ca sāmidhenīnām iṣṭi paśubandheṣu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718737_1]
vacanāt anyat | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718738_1]
kāmyāsu upāṃśu haviḥ tā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718739_1]
anukrāmantaḥ ca vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 16 718740_1]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17}
codanāprakaraṇe haviṣāṃ pratīkagrahaṇam yājyāpuronuvākyānāṃ na ced anyo 'rthasaṃyogaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 1]
dviprabhṛtiṣu codanānupūrvyeṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 2]
daivatena | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 3]
liṅgena ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 4]
upasṛṣṭāsu devatāsv anadhigacchaṃs talliṅge daivatena tuṣyet | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 5]
upasṛṣṭāstu nigacchanti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 6]
abhīkṣṇaṃ caikaikasyai devatāyai haviś codyate tatra ye prathamopadiṣṭe yājyāpuronuvākye te sarvatra pratīyāt | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 7]
na ceṣṭayaḥ pṛthaktvataḥ śakyāḥ parisaṃkhyātum | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 8]
tatrānādiṣṭayājyāpuronuvākyāsu gāyatrītriṣṭubhau taddevate parīcchet | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 9]
uṣṇigbṛhatyau vā parihāpya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 10]
varṣīyasī tu yājyā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 11]
same vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 12]
yatraiteṣām lakṣaṇānām kiṃcit syāt | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 13]
huve havāmahe śrudhy āgahy edaṃ barhir niṣīda devatānām iti puronuvākyālakṣaṇāni | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 14]
addhi piba juṣasva matsvāvṛṣāyasva vīhi pra devatānām iti yājyālakṣaṇāni | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 15]
purastāllakṣaṇā puronuvākyā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 16]
upariṣṭāllakṣaṇā yājyā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 17]
anadhigacchaṃs taddevate namrābhyāṃ yajet | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 18]
imam ā śṛṇudhī havaṃ yat tvā gīrbhir havāmahe | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 19.1]
edaṃ barhir niṣīda naḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 19.2]
stīrṇaṃ barhir ānuṣag ā sadetopeḍānā iha no 'dya gaccha | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 19.3]
aheḍanā manasedaṃ juṣasva vīhi havyaṃ prayatam āhutaṃ naḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 19.4]
ity ūheddvidevatabahudevateṣu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 19.5]
prākṛtīr vābhisaṃnamet prākṛtīr vābhisaṃnamet | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 1, 17 20]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 1}
vasante brāhmaṇasyāgnyādheyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 1 1]

varṣāsu vaiśyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 1 3]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2}
atheṣṭikālāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 1]
sadyo dvādaśāhe māsartau saṃvatsare vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 2]
agnaye pavamānāyeṣṭiḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 3]
paurṇamāsīvikāraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 4]
agna āyūṃṣy agne pavasva | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 5]
taṃ hi śaśvanta īḍate te syāma ye 'gnaya iti sviṣṭakṛtaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 6]
agnaye ca pāvakāyāgnaye ca śucaye dvitīyā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 7]
amāvāsyāvikāraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 8]
agne pāvaka sa saḥ pāvaka | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 9]
agniḥ śucivratatama ud agne śucayaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 10]
agnim agniṃ havīmabhir agnināgniḥ samidhyata iti sviṣṭakṛtaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 11]
aditaye tṛtīyā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 12]
tvam agne saprathāḥ soma yās ta iti sadvantāvājyabhāgau | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 13]
uta tvām adite mahi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 14.1]
mahīm ū ṣu mātaraṃ suvratānāmṛtasya patnīm avase huvema | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 14.2]
tuvikṣatrām ajarantīm urūcīṃ suśarmāṇam aditiṃ supraṇītim | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 14.3]
preddho 'gna imo 'gna iti virājau sviṣṭakṛtaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 2 15]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 8}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 10}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 11}
dakṣiṇatonyāyaṃ yajamānam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 11 1]

ambha sthāmbho vo bhakṣīya maha stha maho vo bhakṣīyorja sthorjaṃ vo bhakṣīya rāyaspoṣa stha rāyaspoṣaṃ vo bhakṣīya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 11 6.1]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12}

upa tvāgna iti tṛcena agne tvaṃ na iti ca dvaipadena gārhapatyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 2]
iḍa ehy adita ehi sūnṛta ehīti gām abhyeti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 3]
kāmyā eta mayi vaḥ kāmadharaṇam iti vatsasya lalāṭam upaspṛśya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 4]
somānaṃ svaraṇam iti tṛcenottarato 'nvāhāryapacanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 5]
antareṇa gārhapatyāhavanīyau māhitraṃ japitvāhavanīyam upatiṣṭhate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 6]
tat savitur vareṇyam kadā cana starīr asi pari te dūlabha iti trir etām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 7]
sarveṣu tu juhvan mahāvyāhṛtibhis tisras tisraḥ samidho 'bhyādadhāty āhavanīye vaikahāvī | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 8]
daivas tantur asy anu tvā rabhe māhaṃ tvad vyavacchitsīty āhavanīyasya dakṣiṇato 'ṅgārān upaspṛśya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 9]
tato 'si tantur asy anu mā saṃtanuhi prajayā paśubhī rāyaspoṣeṇa suprajāstvena suvīryeṇa mānuṣas tantur asy anu mā rabhasva mā tvaṃ mad vyavacchitthā asāv iti jyeṣṭhasya putrasya nāmābhivyāhṛtya yāvanto vā bhavanti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 10]
ātmano 'jātaputraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 11]
satyenāvabhṛtham abhyavaimy apsu vratam ity ācamya vācaṃ visṛjate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 12 12]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 13}
atha prātaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 13 1]
bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ suprajāḥ prajābhir bhūyāsaṃ supoṣaḥ poṣaiḥ suvīro vīrair abhayaṃ te 'bhayaṃ no 'stu manasā tvopatiṣṭhe lokam upaimi svaś cety āhavanīyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 13 2]
atraiva tiṣṭhann itarau | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 13 3]
abhayaṃ te 'bhayaṃ no 'stu vācā tvopatiṣṭhe prajām upaimi paśūṃśceti gārhapatyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 13 4]
abhayaṃ te 'bhayaṃ no 'stu prāṇena tvopatiṣṭhe vyānam upaimyāyuś cety anvāhāryapacanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 13 5]
abhayaṃ vo 'bhayaṃ no 'stu kāmena va upatiṣṭhe vittim upaimi bhūtiṃ ceti sarvān | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 13 6]
samānaṃ samitprabhṛty ā vratasya visarjanāt | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 13 7]
anena vaiva sāyaṃ prātaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 13 8]
anupasthānaṃ vā prātaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 13 9]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14}
pravatsyann agnīn samīkṣate 'bhayaṃ vo 'bhayaṃ no 'stv iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 1]
narya prajāṃ me pāhi mānuṣān mā bhayāt pāhīti gārhapatyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 2]
atharya pituṃ me pāhi pitryān mā bhayāt pāhīty anvāhāryapacanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 3]
tam uttareṇa gatvā śaṃsya paśūn me pāhi daivān mā bhayāt pāhīty āhavanīyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 4]
annam annam iti trīṇi padāny abhyuddhṛtyā sakāśād vāgyamanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 5]
agnyupasthānasyānarthaluptaṃ pravasañjapet | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 6]
yājamānaṃ ca parvaṇi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 7]
anapetaṃ hi kāraṇam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 8]
saṃdhivelayor vācamya vācaṃ yatvā punar ācamya mahāvyāhṛtibhir visargaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 9]
cakṣurviṣaye 'gnīnāṃ vācaṃ yacchet | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 10]
proṣyāyan | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 14 11]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15}
tathā caiva samīkṣaṇam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 1]
āganma vṛtrahantamam asmabhyaṃ vasuvittamam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 2.1]
agne saṃrāḍ abhi dyumnam abhi saha ā yacchasva | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 2.2]
śaṃsya paśūn me 'jugupas tān me pāhy eva daivān mā bhayād ajugupas tasmān mā pāhy evety āhavanīyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 2.3]
tṛṇāpacayanaṃ samidādhānaṃ ca sarveṣu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 3]
ayam agniḥ purīṣyo rayimān puṣṭivardhanaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 4.1]
agne purīṣyābhi dyumnam abhi saha ā yacchasva | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 4.2]
atharya pituṃ me 'jugupas taṃ me pāhyeva pitryān mā bhayād ajugupas tasmān mā pāhy evety anvāhāryapacanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 4.3]
ayam agnir gṛhapatir gārhapatyāt prajāyā vasuvittamaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 5.1]
agne gṛhapate 'bhi dyumnam abhi saha ā yacchasva | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 5.2]
narya prajāṃ me 'jugupas tāṃ me pāhy eva mānuṣān mā bhayād ajugupas tasmān mā pāhy eveti gārhapatyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 5.3]
vyaveto 'gnīn pravasati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 6]
tena caiva utsṛjyate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 15 7]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 16}
vāstoṣpatīyaṃ dhrauvye daśarātrāvarārdhe samprayāteṣu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 16 1]
agniṣṭhasya dakṣiṇe yukta upohya cīvaraṃ vāstoṣpate pratijānīhītyanūcya vāstoṣpate śagmayeti yajati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 16 2]
hute cānāhitaṃ tyajet | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 16 3]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 17}
samārohayamāṇo gārhapatye pāṇī pratitapya prāṇān saṃmṛśaty ehi me prāṇān āroheti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 17 1]
sakṛt sakṛn mantreṇa dvirdvis tūṣṇīm | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 17 2]
ayaṃ te yonir iti vāraṇī pratitapati | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 17 3]
sakṛt sakṛn mantreṇa dvir dvis tūṣṇīm | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 17 4]
evam āhavanīyāt | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 17 5]
nityadhṛtād anyasmin | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 17 6]
anastamite ca manthanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 2, 17 7]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 2}

āhavanīye daśamīṃ samastābhiḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 2 6]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 3}
piṇḍapitṛyajño 'parāhṇe 'māvāsyāyām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 3 1]

purastācchūrpe sthālīm | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 3 5]
ācya savyaṃ jānu nīcā muṣṭinā vrīhīn gṛhṇāti pitṝn dhyāyan | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 3 6]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4}
agnaye kavyavāhanāya svāhā somāya pitṛmate svāhā yamāyāṅgirasvate pitṛmate svāheti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 1]
mekṣaṇam anuprahṛtya dakṣiṇā dakṣiṇāgner apahatā asurā rakṣāṃsi vediṣada iti sphyenonmṛjyābhyukṣya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 2.1]
ye rūpāṇi pratimuñcamānā asurāḥ santaḥ svadhayā caranti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 2.2]
parāpuro nipuro ye bharanty agniṣṭāṃllokāt praṇudāty asmāt | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 2.3]
ity ulmukam unmṛṣṭasya dakṣiṇārdhe nidhāya mūle kuśān sakṛllūnān unmṛṣṭe nidhāyāsāvavanenikṣva ye ca tvām atrānv iti pitur nāmādiśya kuśeṣv apo niṣiñcaty avācīnapāṇinā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 2.4]
evaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pitāmahasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 3]
prapitāmahasya ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 4]
asāv etat te ye ca tvām atrānv iti piṇḍān yathāvanejitaṃ nidhāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 5]
ubhāv ekasmin pitṛbhede | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 6]
na jīvapitur asti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 7]
na jīvāntarhitāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 8]
tebhyo vā pitā tebhyaḥ putraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 9]
homāntaṃ vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 10]
atra pitaro mādayadhvaṃ yathābhāgaṃ pitara āvṛṣāyadhvam iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 11]
udaṅ paryāvṛtya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 12]
trirātamanādāsitvā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 13]

tathaiva avanejya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 4 15]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5}
namo vaḥ pitaro jīvāya namo vaḥ pitaraḥ śoṣāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 1.1]
namo vaḥ pitaro ghorāya namo vaḥ pitaro rasāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 1.2]
namo vaḥ pitaro balāya namo vaḥ pitaro mṛtyave | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 1.3]
namo vaḥ pitaro manyave namo vaḥ pitaraḥ svadhāyai | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 1.4]
namo vaḥ pitaraḥ pitaro namo vaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 1.5]
ye 'tra pitaraḥ pitaraḥ stha yūyaṃ teṣāṃ śreṣṭhā bhūyāstha | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 1.6]

yātra pitaraḥ svadhā yuṣmākaṃ sā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 1.8]
ya iha pitara edhatur asmākaṃ sa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 1.9]
gṛhān naḥ pitaro datteti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 1.10]
etad vaḥ pitaro vāso vadhvaṃ pitara iti trīṇi sūtrāṇy upanyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 2]
ūrjaṃ vahantīr amṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ payaḥ kīlālaṃ parisrutam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 3.1]
svadhā stha tarpayata naḥ pitṝn ity udakaśeṣaṃ ninīya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 3.2]
avaghrāya piṇḍān | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 4]
avadhāya prāśnīyāt | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 5]
brāhmaṇāya vā dadyāt | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 6]
apo vābhyavaharet | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 7]
madhyamapiṇḍaṃ patnī putrakāmā prāśnīyāt | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 8.1]

yatheha puruṣo 'sat | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 8.3]
iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 5 8.4]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 6}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 7}
praṇītākāle vāgyamanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 7 1]
haviṣkṛtā visargaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 7 2]

mitrasya tvā cakṣuṣā pratīkṣa iti prāśitraṃ pratīkṣya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 7 4]
devasya tvā savituḥ prasave 'śvinor bāhubhyāṃ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ pratigṛhṇāmīti pratigṛhya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 7 5]

brahman prasthāsyāmīty uktaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 7 16]
deva savitar etaṃ te yajñaṃ prāhur bṛhaspataye brahmaṇe tena yajñam ava tena yajñapatiṃ tena mām ava devena savitrā prasūta iti japitvā oṃ pratiṣṭheti prasauti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 7 17]
praṇītāsu vimuktāsūtsarjanaṃ brahmaṇaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 7 18]
prāśanaṃ brahmabhāgasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 7 19]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 8}
adabdhena tvā cakṣuṣā avapaśyāmi rāyaspoṣāya suprajāstvāya suvīryāyāgner jihvāsi suhūr devebhyo dhāmne dhāmne me bhava yajuṣe yajuṣa ity ājyam avekṣate patnī | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 8 1]
tejo 'si śukram asy amṛtam asi vaiśvadevam asīty āsannaṃ vedau yajamānaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 8 2]
dhruvā asadannṛtasya yonau sukṛtasya loke tā viṣṇo pāhi pāhi yajñaṃ pāhi yajñapatim ity āsannāni havīṃṣyabhimṛśya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 8 3.1]
pāhi māṃ yajñanyam ity ātmānam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 8 3.2]
vṛṣṭir asi pāpmanāṃ me vṛśca vidyāsi vidya me pāpmānam ity ācamya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 8 4.1]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 9}

prajāpater bhāgo 'sy ūrjasvān payasvān akṣitir asi mā me kṣeṣṭhā amutrāmuṣmiṃlloka iha cety anvāhāryam abhimṛśya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 9 4]
anuyājeṣv iṣṭeṣu vyūhitasrucāv agner agnīṣomayor ujjitim anūjjeṣaṃ vājasya mā prasavena prohāmīty uttānena dakṣiṇena juhūṃ prācīm agnir agnīṣomau tam apanudantu yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo vājasya enaṃ prasavena apohāmīti nīcā savyenopabhṛtaṃ pratīcīm | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 9 5]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 10}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 11}

paraitu mṛtyur amṛtaṃ ma ā gād vaivasvato no 'bhayam kṛṇotu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 5.2]
parṇaṃ vanaspater iva abhi naḥ śīyatāṃ rayiḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 5.3]
sacatāṃ na śacīpatiḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 5.4]
yāś cāruṇe daśānvādhāna iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 5.5]
dvādaśa hutvā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 6.1]
yathāhānīti dakṣiṇam anvaṃsaṃ dvābhyāṃ samīkṣya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 6.2]
añjanaṃ sarpiṣā saṃninīya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 6.3]
kuśaiḥ strīṇām akṣīṇy anaktīm ā nārīr iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 6.4]
sakṛt sakṛn mantreṇa dvir dvis tūṣṇīm | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 6.5]
uttiṣṭha brahmaṇaspata iti dvābhyāṃ brāhmaṇasya dakṣiṇaṃ bāhum anvārabdhān uttiṣṭhato 'numantrayate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 7]
anaḍuho vā puccham | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 8]
anaḍvān ahataṃ vāsaḥ kāṃsyaś ca dakṣiṇā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 9]
dakṣiṇato vittaṃ ni vartadhvam iti sūktena pratyenāḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ triḥ paryeti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 10]
pratyenasi paridhikarma | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 16 11]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 17}
rudraṃ gavā yajate svastyayanāya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 17 1]
śūlagava ity ācakṣate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 17 2]
śuddhapakṣa upoṣya puṣye nakṣatre prāgudīcyāṃ diśi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 17 3]
agniṃ mathitvā prāñcaṃ praṇīya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 17 4]

paryagnikṛtam udañcaṃ nayanti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 17 10]

yat paśur māyum akṛta uro vā padbhir āhate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 17 12.1]
agnir mā tasmād enaso jātavedāḥ pra muñcatu | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 17 12.2]
svāheti ravamāṇe juhoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 17 12.3]
vapām uddhṛtya prakṣālya pūrve 'gnau śrapayitvābhighāryodvāsya śivaṃ śivam iti triḥ paryukṣyājyāhutīr juhoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 17 13]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 18}
yā tiraścī ni padyate 'haṃ vidharaṇīti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 18 1.1]

svāhā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 18 1.3]
yasyedaṃ sarvaṃ tam imaṃ havāmahe | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 18 2.1]

anupraharati palāśāni | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 18 5.7]
vapāśrapaṇyau ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 18 6]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 19}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 20}
bhūpate bhuvapate bhuvanapate bhūtapate bhūtānāṃ pate mahato bhūtasya pate mṛḍa no dvipade ca catuṣpade ca paśave mṛḍa naś ca dvipadaś ca catuṣpadaś ca paśūn yo 'smān dveṣṭi yaṃ ca vayaṃ dviṣmo durāpūro 'si sacchāyo 'dhināmena | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 20 1.1]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 21}

yaśase brahmavarcasāyeti vikāraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 21 7.2]
pratigṛhya savye pāṇau kṛtvāṅguṣṭhenopakaniṣṭhikayā ca pūrvārdhād upahatya pūrvārdhe kāṃsyasya nilimpati vasavas tvāgnirājāno bhakṣayantv iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 21 8]
pitaras tvā yamarājāno bhakṣayantv iti dakṣiṇārdhāddakṣiṇārdhe | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 21 9]
ādityās tvā varuṇarājāno bhakṣayantv iti paścārdhāt paścārdhe | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 21 10]
rudrās tvendrarājāno bhakṣayantv ity uttarārdhād uttarārdhe | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 21 11]

sakṛt sakṛn mantreṇa dvir dvis tūṣṇīm | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 21 13]

gaur ity ukta oṃ kuruta | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 4, 21 23]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 5, 1}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 5, 6}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 5, 8}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 6, 3}
asyāṃ me prācyāṃ diśi sūryaś ca candraś cādhipatī sūryaś ca candraśca maitasyai diśaḥ pātāṃ sūryaṃ ca candraṃ ca sa devatānām ṛcchatu yo no 'to 'bhidāsatīti prācīm | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 6, 3 1]

asyāṃ me pratīcyāṃ diśi mitraś ca varuṇaś cādhipatī mitraś ca varuṇaś ca maitasyai diśaḥ pātāṃ mitraṃ ca varuṇaṃ ca sa devatānāmṛcchatu yo no 'to 'bhidāsatīti pratīcīm | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 6, 3 3]
asyāṃ ma udīcyāṃ diśi somaś ca rudraś cādhipatī somaśca rudraś ca maitasyai diśaḥ pātāṃ somaṃ ca rudraṃ ca sa devatānāmṛcchatu yo no 'to 'bhidāsatīti savyāvṛd udīcīm | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 6, 3 4]
asyāṃ ma ūrdhvāyāṃ diśi bṛhaspatiś cendraś cādhipatī bṛhaspatiś cendraś ca maitasyai diśaḥ pātāṃ bṛhaspatiṃ cendraṃ ca sa devatānāmṛcchatu yo no 'to 'bhidāsatīti prāṅūrdhvām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 6, 3 5]
asmin me 'ntarikṣe vāyuś ca vṛṣṭiś cādhipatī vāyuś ca vṛṣṭiś ca maitasyai diśaḥ pātāṃ vāyuṃ ca vṛṣṭiṃ ca sa devatānāmṛcchatu yo no 'to 'bhidāsatīty antarikṣam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 6, 3 6]
asyāṃ me pṛthivyām agniś cānnaṃ cādhipatī agniś cānnaṃ ca maitasyai diśaḥ pātām agniṃ ca annaṃ ca sa devatānāmṛcchatu yo no 'to 'bhidāsatīti pṛthivīm | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 6, 3 7]

dharmaḥ indraḥ iti daśame | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 2 720196_1]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 4}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 5}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 6}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 7}

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 10}

tataṃ me yajñena vardhatety ārbhavajātavedasīye dvitīyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 20 15]
trirātre ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 20 16]
abhijidviśvajitau caturviṃśamahāvrate goāyuṣī vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 20 17]
yaddvividhaṃ taddvirātreṇāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 20 18]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21}
atha yat trividhaṃ tat trirātreṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 1]
trayo vā ime lokās trīṇi jyotīṃṣi tripavaṇo yajñaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 2.1]
tad yat kiṃca trividham adhidaivatam adhyātmaṃ tat sarvam enenāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 2.2]
trivṛtprabhṛtayas trayaḥ stomāḥ prathamasyāhnaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 3]
pañcadaśaprabhṛtayo dvitīyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 4]
ṣoḍaśaṃ brahmaṇa ājyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 5]
ekaviṃśaprabhṛtayas tṛtīyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 6]
agniṣṭomaḥ prathamam ahaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 7]
ukthyaṃ dvitīyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 8]
atirātras tṛtīyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 9]
rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ prathamasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 10]
vāmadevyaṃ dvitīyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 11]
bṛhat tṛtīyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 12]
ayaṃ vai loko rathantaram | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 13]
antarikṣaloko vāmadevyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 14]
asau loko bṛhat | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 15]
eteṣām eva lokānām āptyai | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 16]
samūḍhād ājyāni | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 17]
madhyamācchandomāt traiṣṭubhaḥ praugo dvitīyasya ahnaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 18]
aryameti marutvatīyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 19]
yaddvitīyasyāhno marutvatīyaṃ tat tṛtīye 'hani karoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 20]
tad imāṃllokān sambhoginaḥ karoti tasmāddhīme lokā anyonyam abhibhuñjantīti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 21]
ahanī vā viparyasyet | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 22]
kas tam indreti sāmapragātho niṣkevalyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 23]
mo ṣu tvā vāghataś caneti stotriyānurūpau pragāthau maitrāvaruṇasya uddhṛtya dvipadām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 24]
kaṃ navya iti kadvān | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 25]
dvitīyād ahnaḥ sūkte | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 26]
astāvi manmobhayaṃ śṛṇavad iti brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 27]
kad ū nv asyeti kadvān | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 28]
śrāyanta iva sūryaṃ śagdhy ū ṣu śacīpata ity acchāvākasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 29]
yad indra prāg apāg udag iti kadvān | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 30]
kayāśubhīyatadidāsīye vā nividdhāne dvitīyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 31]
anucaraprabhṛti ṣaṣṭhāt tṛtīyasavanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 21 32]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22}
eṣo nvai sahasrastotriyo yena prajāpatir ayajata | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 1]
etam eva gargatrirātra ity ācakṣate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 2]
dvitīyo 'śvitrirātraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 3]
madhyame 'hanyaśvam ālabhante | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 4]
adhrigāv aśvastomīyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 5]
tṛtīyaś chandomaḥ pavamānaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 6]
parākaś caturthaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 7]
pṛṣṭhyastomais triṣṭomāni trīṇi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 8]
eṣa u parākaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 9]
etenāsmāllokāt prajigāṃsan yajeta | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 10]
pratiṣṭhākāmasya dvaiparāka ity āhuḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 11]
yā hy ekā jagatī te dve gāyatryau | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 12]
ayaṃ loko gāyatras tad asmiṃlloke pratitiṣṭhati pratiṣṭhāyām apracyutyām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 13]
jyotir gaur āyur iti kusurubindutrirātraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 14]
trīṇi śatāni prathame 'han dadāti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 15]
trayastriṃśataṃ pañca kalāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 16]
evaṃ dvitīya evaṃ tṛtīye | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 17]
tatkalā sahasratamyā goḥ pariśiṣyate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 18]
tām anyayā gavā niṣkrīyāmākurvīta | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 19]
amākāryety āhur yajamānasya eva sambhūtyā iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 20]
yāyantīnāṃ prathamoparamet sā syād ity āhuḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 21]
tad apracyutyai rūpam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 22]
yā saṃtiṣṭhantīnāṃ prathamopaviśet sā syād ity āhuḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 23]
tat pratiṣṭhāyai rūpam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 24]
yādyaśvīnā sā syād ityāhuḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 25]
tat prajātyai rūpam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 26]
yā sattamā sā syād ity āhuḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 27]
sattamām amākaravā iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 28]
sarvavedatrirātre triśukriyo brahmā yasyobhayataḥ śrotriyās tripuruṣam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 29]
yat trividhaṃ tat trirātreṇāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 22 30]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23}
atha yaccaturvidhaṃ taccatūrātreṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 1]
catuṣṭayā vai paśavaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 2]
atho catuṣpādāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 3]
tad yat kiṃ ca caturvidham adhidaivatam adhyātmaṃ tat sarvam enenāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 4]
trivṛt prathamam ahaḥ pañcadaśaṃ dvitīyaṃ saptadaśaṃ tṛtīyam ekaviṃśaṃ caturtham | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 5]
te vā ete catvāraḥ stomā nānāvīryā yajñakratavas tena hāsya catvāro vīrā nānāvīryāḥ prajāyām ājāyante ya evaṃ veda | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 6]
eṣo nvai jamadagneś catūrātraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 7]
athaivātreś caturvīraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 8]
trivṛt prathamasyāhnaḥ prātaḥsavanaṃ pañcadaśo mādhyaṃdinaḥ saptadaśaṃ tṛtīyasavanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 9]
pañcadaśaṃ dvitīyasyāhnaḥ prātaḥsavanaṃ saptadaśo mādhyaṃdina ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 10]
saptadaśaṃ tṛtīyasyāhnaḥ prātaḥsavanam ekaviṃśo mādhyaṃdinas triṇavaṃ tṛtīyasavanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 11]
ekaviṃśaṃ caturthasyāhnaḥ prātaḥsavanaṃ triṇavo mādhyaṃdinas trayastriṃśaṃ tṛtīyasavanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 12]
te vā ekaikaṃ stomam utsṛjanto yantyekaikaṃ prajanayantaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 13]
tena hāsya catvāro vīrā nānāvīryāḥ prajāyām ājāyante | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 14.1]
vīro hi stomaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 14.2]
tasya śastram | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 15]
rathantaraṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ prathamasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 16]
sajanīyaṃ niṣkevalyam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 17]
kayāśubhīyatadidāsīye vā nividdhāne dvitīyasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 18]
tṛtīye vairūpapṛṣṭhe vairājāt tṛtīyasavanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 19]
caturthe vairājapṛṣṭhe vairūpāt tṛtīyasavanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 20]
prākṛto vā atirātraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 21]
taṃ vaiśvānara ity ācakṣate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 22]
abhijid ābhiplavikānāṃ caturthaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 23]
viśvajid itareṣām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 24]
vaiśvānaro mahāvrataṃ vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 25]
yaccaturvidhaṃ taccatūrātreṇa āpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 23 26]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24}
atha yat pañcavidhaṃ tat pañcarātreṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 1]
pañcapadā paṅktiḥ pāṅkto vai yajñas tad yat kiṃ ca pañcavidham adhidaivatam adhyātmaṃ tat sarvam enenāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 2]
trivṛt prathamam ahaḥ pañcadaśaṃ dvitīyam ekaviṃśaṃ tṛtīyaṃ saptadaśaṃ caturthaṃ catuṣṭomo 'tirātra uttamam ahaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 3]
tad vā idam āsām eva rūpeṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 4]
iyam eva trivṛto rūpeṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 5]
iyaṃ pañcadaśasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 6]
iyam ekaviṃśasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 7]
iyaṃ saptadaśasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 8]
ayaṃ catuṣṭomasyātirātrasya | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 9]
tad yad ekaviṃśastomānāṃ varṣiṣṭhas tasmād iyam āsāṃ varṣiṣṭhā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 10]
atha yaccatuṣṭomo 'tirātra uttamam ahas tasmād ayam aṅguṣṭhaḥ sarvā aṅgulīḥ pratyeti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 11]
tasya śastram | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 12]
tryahaś caturtham ābhiplavikam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 13]
pañcamasya ca dve savane ṣaṣṭhāt pṛṣṭhyasya pañcame tṛtīyasavanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 14]
pañca vā ābhiplavikāni | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 15]
uttamāt pañcame tṛtīyasavanam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 16]
abhijid ābhiplavikānāṃ caturthaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 17]
viśvajid itareṣām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 18]
vaiśvānaraś ca mahāvrataṃ vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 19]
ubhayor vā abhijiccaturtho viśvajit pañcamaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 20]
yat pañcavidhaṃ tat pañcarātreṇāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 24 21]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 25}
atha yat ṣaḍvidhaṃ tat ṣaḍrātreṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 25 1]
ṣaḍ vā ṛtavaḥ ṣaṭ stomās tad yat kiṃ ca ṣaḍvidham adhidaivatam adhyātmaṃ tat sarvam enenāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 25 2]
tryaho 'bhijid viśvajitau vaiśvānaraś ca mahāvrataṃ vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 25 3]
anantaraṃ vābhijito mahāvratam | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 25 4]
viśvajit ṣaṣṭhaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 25 5]
pṛṣṭhyo 'bhiplavo vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 25 6]
yat ṣaḍvidhaṃ tat ṣaḍrātreṇāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 25 7]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26}
atha yat saptavidhaṃ tat saptarātreṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 1]
sapta prāṇāḥ sapta chandāṃsi tad yat kiṃ ca saptavidham adhidaivatam adhyātmaṃ tat sarvam enenāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 2]
tryaho 'bhijid viśvajitau mahāvrataṃ vaiśvānaraś ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 3]
atha saṃvatsarasya pravalhaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 4]
prākṛto 'gniṣṭomaś caturviṃśam abhijid viṣuvān viśvajin mahāvrataṃ vaiśvānaraś ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 5]
eṣo nvai saptarṣīṇāṃ saptarātraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 6]
etam eva janakasaptarātra ity ācakṣate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 7]
abhijid ābhiplavikānāṃ saptamaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 8]
viśvajid itareṣām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 9]
vaiśvānaro mahāvrataṃ vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 10]
yat saptavidhaṃ tat saptarātreṇāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 26 11]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 27}
atha yad aṣṭavidhaṃ tad aṣṭarātreṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 27 1]
aṣṭau vasavo 'ṣṭākṣarā gāyatrī tad yat kiṃ cāṣṭavidham adhidaivatam adhyātmaṃ tat sarvam enenāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 27 2]
abhijid ābhiplavikānāṃ saptamaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 27 3]
viśvajid itareṣām | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 27 4]
vaiśvānaraś ca mahāvrataṃ vā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 27 5]
ubhayor vābhijit saptamo viśvajid aṣṭamaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 27 6]

{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 28}
atha yannavavidhaṃ tannavarātreṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 28 1]
catasro diśaś catasro 'vāntaradiśa ūrdhveyaṃ navamī diṅ navākṣarā bṛhatī tad yat kiṃ ca navavidham adhidaivatam adhyātmaṃ tat sarvam anenāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 28 2]
ṣaḍaho 'bhijid viśvajitau vaiśvānaraś ca mahāvrataṃ vānantaraṃ vābhijito mahāvrataṃ viśvajin navamaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 28 3]
jyotir agniṣṭomo gaur ukthya āyur atirātras trir etam upayanti śalalīpiśaṅga ity ācakṣate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 28 4]
yan navavidhaṃ tan navarātreṇāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 28 5]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29}
atha yaddaśavidhaṃ taddaśarātreṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 1]
daśākṣarā virāḍ annaṃ virāṭ tad yat kiṃ ca daśavidham adhidaivatam adhyātmaṃ tat sarvam enenāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 2]
adhyardho 'bhiplavo nava vāgniṣṭomāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 3]
daśarātraḥ saṃsthāvikṛtaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 4]
vaiśvānaraś ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 5]
etena ha jalo jātūkarṇya iṣṭvā trayāṇāṃ nigusthānāṃ purodhāṃ prāpa kāśyavaidehayoḥ kausalyasya ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 6]
tasya ha tacchvetaketuḥ śriyam abhidhyāya pitaram adhyūhe palita yajñakāmān yān vā u śriyā yaśasā samardhayituṃ vettha no ātmānam iti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 7]
taṃ ha uvāca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 8.1]
mā maivaṃ putra voco yajñakratur eva me vijñāto 'bhūt tam eva etat kṛtsnake brahmabandhau vyajijñāsiṣi | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 8.2]
tad u kila tathaivāsa yathaivainaṃ provāca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 9]
sa eṣa purodhākāmasya yajñaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 10]
pra purodhām āpnoti ya evaṃ veda | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 11]
catuṣṭomāt samūḍhāt trikakudaḥ śastram | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 12]
atha mahātrikakudaś ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 13]
chandomatrikakudaś ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 14]
agniṣṭud indrastud vaiśvadevastut pṛṣṭhyo vaiśvānaraś ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 15]
ṣaḍaho 'bhijid aśvajitau mahāvrataṃ vaiśvānaraś ca | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 16]
prākṛto 'gniṣṭomo navamo 'ṣṭamo vā viśvajiddaśamaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 17]
yaddaśavidhaṃ taddaśarātreṇāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 29 18]
{ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30}
atha yad ekādaśavidhaṃ tad ekādaśarātreṇa | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30 1]
ekādaśākṣarā triṣṭup traiṣṭubhāḥ paśavas tad yat kiṃ caikādaśavidham adhidaivatam adhyātmaṃ tat sarvam enenāpnoti | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30 2]
vyūḍhachandā daśarātraḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30 3]
viśvajid ekādaśaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30 4]
taṃ pauṇḍarīka ity ācakṣate | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30 5]
ayutaṃ dakṣiṇā | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30 6]
aśvasahasram ekādaśam ity eke | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30 7]
ukto dvādaśāhaḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30 8]
ta ete purastād agniṣṭomā upariṣṭād atirātrā uttarottariṇa ekottarā ahīnāḥ | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30 9]
uttarottariṇīm eva tacchriyaṃ virājam annādyamāpnoti ya evaṃ veda ya evaṃ veda | [ŚāṅkhŚS, 16, 30 10]
